	 WITH (  PAD_INDEX = OFF ,FILLFACTOR = 100  ,SORT_IN_TEMPDB = OFF , IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF , STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF , ONLINE = OFF , ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON , ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON  )
	 ON [PRIMARY ] ;
 CREATE NONCLUSTERED INDEX IDX_WfANtype ON LatidataSQL.dbo.tblWfActionNotify (  WfANtype ASC  )  
	 WITH (  PAD_INDEX = OFF ,FILLFACTOR = 100  ,SORT_IN_TEMPDB = OFF , IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF , STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF , ONLINE = OFF , ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON , ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON  )
	 ON [PRIMARY ] ;


-- dbo.qryJobExport source

AS

	SELECT *
	FROM tblJobs;


-- dbo.qryResources source

ALTER   VIEW dbo.qryResources
AS
	SELECT TOP(100) PERCENT 
		E.[Employee Code] AS [Resource Code], 
		E.[First Name] AS Description, 
		E.Surname AS Model, 
		E.curSalary AS [Purchase Price], 
		E.[Birth Date] AS [Purchase Date], 
		E.[Starting Date] AS [Sold Date], 
		E.Street AS [Storage Address], 
		E.*
	FROM tblEmployees AS E
	WHERE (((E.Status)='Resource'));

-- dbo.vwLA_qryJobCaptain source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[vwLA_qryJobCaptain]
AS
SELECT     J.[Job Number], J.[Job Description], LTRIM(RTRIM(ISNULL(PM.[First Name], N'') + ' ' + ISNULL(PM.Surname, N''))) AS Contact
FROM         dbo.tblJobs AS J LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.tblEmployees AS PM ON J.strCaptainCode = PM.[Employee Code];


-- dbo.vwLA_qryJobHasInvoice source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[vwLA_qryJobHasInvoice]
AS

	SELECT tblJobs.[Job Number], Count(tblClientsInvoices.lngInvoiceNo) AS InvoiceCount
	FROM tblJobs LEFT JOIN tblClientsInvoices ON tblJobs.[Job Number] = tblClientsInvoices.txtJobNumber
	GROUP BY tblJobs.[Job Number];


-- dbo.vwLA_qryJobWorkflowCurrent source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[vwLA_qryJobWorkflowCurrent]
AS

	SELECT TOP(100) PERCENT
		R1.strJobReference,
		WfDate = R2.dteRegisterDate,
		WfStage = R2.strRe,
		WfDetail = CONVERT(NVARCHAR(255), R2.Details),
		WfAssigned = R2.strFrom,
		WfNotify = R2.EmpNotify
	FROM tblRegister R1
	CROSS APPLY (
		SELECT TOP 1 * FROM tblRegister R2a
		WHERE
				R2a.strJobReference = R1.strJobReference
			AND R2a.strRegisterType = 'Workflow'
		ORDER BY R2a.dteRegisterDate DESC, R2a.Counter DESC
	) AS R2
	
	GROUP BY 
		R1.strJobReference, R2.dteRegisterDate, R2.strRe, CONVERT(NVARCHAR(255), R2.Details), R2.strFrom, R2.EmpNotify;

                      dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDKey AS Expr1, dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDSrchStr, dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDType, dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDPlans, dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDComments, 
                      dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDF1, dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDF2, dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDF3, dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDF4, dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDF5, dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDF6, 
                      dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDF7, dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDF8, dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDF9, dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDF10, dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDF11, dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDF12, 
                      dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDF13, dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDF14, dbo.tblLegalDesc.LDF15, dbo.tblLegalDesc.upsize_ts AS Expr2

-- dbo.vwLA_qryQuoteAddress source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[vwLA_qryQuoteAddress]
AS
SELECT     dbo.tblJobs.[Job Number], dbo.tblJobs.InstructingPersonId, dbo.tblClientsContacts.ContactSalutation, dbo.tblClientsContacts.ContactGivenName, 
                      dbo.tblClientsContacts.ContactSurname, dbo.tblJobs.Client, dbo.tblClients.ynCompany, dbo.tblClients.[Company Name], dbo.tblClients.[Postal Address], 
                      dbo.tblClients.[Postal Suburb], dbo.tblClients.[Postal PostCode], dbo.tblClients.[Postal State], dbo.tblClients.PostalCountry
FROM         dbo.tblClients RIGHT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.tblJobs LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.tblClientsContacts ON dbo.tblJobs.InstructingPersonId = dbo.tblClientsContacts.ContactID ON dbo.tblClients.[Client Code] = dbo.tblJobs.Client;

-- dbo.vwTimesheet source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[vwTimesheet]
AS
SELECT
		tTimesheets.[Timesheet Number] AS TimesheetId,
		tTimesheets.[Date] AS [Date],
		tTimesheets.[Status] AS StatusCode,
		tTimesheets.[Work Description] AS [Description],
		tTimesheets.[Employee Code] AS EmpCode,
		tTimesheets.[Job Number] AS JobNumber,
		tTimesheets.[Job Description] AS JobDesc,
		tTimesheets.[strJobNoteRef] AS CBCode,
		tCBCodes.[CBDesc] AS CBDesc,
		tTimesheets.[Work Type] AS WorkTypeCode,
		tWorkTypes.[Work Type Description] AS WorkTypeDesc,
		tTimesheets.[strTaskType] AS TaskTypeCode,
		tLookups.[strDescription] AS TaskTypeDesc,
		tTimesheets.[PayTypeKey] AS PayTypeKey,
		tPayType.[PayTypeCode] AS PayTypeCode, 
		tPayType.[PayTypeDesc] AS PayTypeDesc, 
		tTimesheets.[tmeStart] AS StartTime,
		tTimesheets.[tmeEnd] AS EndTime,
		tTimesheets.[Hours Worked] AS Quantity,
		tTimesheets.[txtUnit] AS Unit,
		tTimesheets.[curCostRate] AS CostRate,
		tTimesheets.[sglFactor] AS Factor,
		tTimesheets.[curCostsExtension] AS Cost,
		tTimesheets.[Hourly Rate] AS ChargeRate,
		tTimesheets.[Extension] AS Charge,
		tTimesheets.[bolDisbursement] AS Disbursement,
		tTimesheets.[bolNonChargeable] AS NonChargeable,
		tTimesheets.[lngInvoiceNo] AS InvoiceNumber,
		TaskCode,
		--TsStatus,
		TsSrc
		
FROM dbo.[tblTimesheets] AS tTimesheets
		LEFT JOIN dbo.tlkpCBCodes AS tCBCodes ON tTimesheets.[strJobNoteRef] = tCBCodes.[CBCode]
		LEFT JOIN dbo.tlkpWorkTypes AS tWorkTypes ON tWorkTypes.[Work Type Code] = tTimesheets.[Work Type]
		LEFT JOIN dbo.tblLookups AS tLookups ON tLookups.[strCode] = tTimesheets.[strTaskType] AND tLookups.[strType] = 'JobNoteType'
		LEFT JOIN dbo.tlkpPayType AS tPayType ON tPayType.[PayTypeKey] = tTimesheets.[PayTypeKey];


-- dbo.zsqmlClientContacts_SQL source

                      ContactMobile, ContactComments, ContactEMail, bolMainContact, strContactUserField1, strContactUserField2, strContactUserField3, strContactUserField4, 
                      strContactUserField5, strContactUserField6, strContactUserField7, strContactUserField8, strContactUserField9, strContactUserField10, ContactSuburb, ContactState, 
                      ContactPostCode, ContactPostalAddress, ContactPostalSuburb, ContactPostalState, ContactPostalPostCode, ContactCountry, ContactPostalCountry, 
                      ContactCompanyName, bolMktContact, bolCurrent, txtRole, upsize_ts
FROM         dbo.tblClientsContacts;


-- dbo.zsqmlClientRef_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlClientRef_SQL]
AS
	SELECT 
		tblClientRefs.ClientRefId, 
		tblClientRefs.JobNo, 
		tblClientRefs.ClientRefType, 
		ClientRefTypeName = (
			ISNULL((
				SELECT [strNewFieldName] FROM zstblCustomFields
				WHERE
						[strDisipline] = ( SELECT TOP 1 [txtDisipline] FROM zstblSetup )
					AND [strFieldName] = 'lblClientRef' + CONVERT(CHAR, tblClientRefs.ClientRefType))
				, 'Client Ref ' + CONVERT(CHAR, tblClientRefs.ClientRefType))
		),
		tblClientRefs.ClientRefNo, 
		tblClientRefs.Status, 
		tblClientRefs.MaxAmt, 
		tblClientRefs.EstHrs, 
		tblClientRefs.Usage
	FROM tblClientRefs;


-- dbo.zsqmlClientsInvoicesDetailsSortBySort_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlClientsInvoicesDetailsSortBySort_SQL]
AS
SELECT     TOP (100) PERCENT dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.cntInvoiceDetNo, dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.lngInvoiceNo, dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.memDetail, 
                      dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.strCBCode, dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.curAmount, dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.Qty, dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.Rate, 
                      dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.Unit, dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.Sort, dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.[Group], dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.IsSubtotal, 
                      dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.GLAccount, dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.taxd_id, dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.taxi_territory, dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.tdcbo_id, 
                      dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.cinv_rate_used, dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.TaxAmount, dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.IncTaxAmount, 
                      dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.strResourceType, dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.JobNo, dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.TaskCode, 
                      dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.PreviousClaim, dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.upsize_ts, dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.GLAcctNo, dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.TaxId, 
                      dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.CurTaxAmt, dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.CurLineAmt, dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.TSGroup, 
                      dbo.tblClientsInvoices.txtJobNumber AS JobNumber
FROM         dbo.tblClientsInvoices INNER JOIN
                      dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails ON dbo.tblClientsInvoices.lngInvoiceNo = dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.lngInvoiceNo
ORDER BY dbo.tblClientsInvoicesDetails.Sort;


-- dbo.zsqmlClients_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlClients_SQL]
AS
SELECT     TOP(100) PERCENT 
	C.*,

	MainContactGivenName = C.[Postal Name],
	MainContactGivenNameInitial = LEFT(C.[Postal Name], 1),
	MainContactSurname = C.[PostalSurname],
	MainContactSurnameInitial = LEFT(C.[PostalSurname], 1),	
	MainContactTitle = C.[PostalTitle],
	MainContactEmail = (SELECT TOP 1 CC.ContactEMail FROM dbo.tblClientsContacts AS CC WHERE CC.ClientId = C.[Client Code] AND CC.bolMainContact = 1),
	MainContactPhone = (SELECT TOP 1 CC.ContactPhone FROM dbo.tblClientsContacts AS CC WHERE CC.ClientId = C.[Client Code] AND CC.bolMainContact = 1),
	MainContactFax = (SELECT TOP 1 CC.ContactFax FROM dbo.tblClientsContacts AS CC WHERE CC.ClientId = C.[Client Code] AND CC.bolMainContact = 1),
	MainContactMobile = (SELECT TOP 1 CC.ContactMobile FROM dbo.tblClientsContacts AS CC WHERE CC.ClientId = C.[Client Code] AND CC.bolMainContact = 1)

FROM dbo.tblClients AS C;


-- dbo.zsqmlDisbursementsSortByDateDesc_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlDisbursementsSortByDateDesc_SQL]
AS
SELECT     TOP (100) PERCENT 
	T.[TimeSheet Number], 
	T.[Employee Code], 
	T.Date, 
	T.[Job Number], 
	T.[Work Type], 
	T.[Hours Worked], 
	T.[Hourly Rate], 
	T.[Work Description], 
	T.Extension, 
	T.[Job Description], 
	T.TDate, 
	T.ApptTime, 
	T.Status, 
	T.ApptDate, 
	T.lngInvoiceNo, 
	T.txtUnit, 
	T.curCostRate, 
	T.curCostsExtension, 
	T.tmeStart, 
	T.tmeEnd, 
	T.strJobNoteRef, 
	T.bolDisbursement, 
    T.bolNonChargeable, 
    T.sglFactor, 
    T.strTaskType, 
    T.PayTypeKey, 
    T.bolShow, 
    T.TaskCode, 
    T.lngInvoiceNoDraft, 
    T.PayExportDate, 
    T.OTclaim, 
    T.upsize_ts, 
    T.InvTSGroup, 
	T.TsSrc, 
	WT.[Work Type Description], 
	WT.[WorkTypeLongDesc]
FROM         dbo.tblTimesheets T
LEFT JOIN tlkpWorkTypes WT ON WT.[Work Type Code] = T.[Work Type]
WHERE     (T.bolDisbursement = 1)
ORDER BY Date DESC;


-- dbo.zsqmlFTDailyRate_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlFTDailyRate_SQL]
AS
	SELECT 
		tblFTdailyRates.SeqNo, 
		tblFTdailyRates.TicketId, 
		tblFTdailyRates.DrItemId, 
		tlkpFTdailyRate.[Desc] AS ItemDesc, 
		tlkpFTdailyRate.WorkType AS ItemWorkType, 
		tblFTdailyRates.ChargeRate, 
		tblFTdailyRates.Qty, 
		[Qty]*[ChargeRate] AS Amount, 
		tblFTdailyRates.OrderNo
	FROM tblFTdailyRates INNER JOIN tlkpFTdailyRate ON tblFTdailyRates.DrItemId = tlkpFTdailyRate.DrItemId;

	SELECT 
		tblFTdisb.SeqNo, 
		tblFTdisb.TicketId, 
		tblFTdisb.WorkType AS DisbWorkType,

-- dbo.zsqmlFTDocument_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlFTDocument_SQL]
AS

	SELECT 
		tblFTdocs.FTdocId, 
		tblFTdocs.TicketId, 
		tblFTdocs.PathFileName AS DocumentFileName, 
		CASE WHEN [bolCurrent] = 1 THEN 'Yes' ELSE 'No' END AS [Current], 
		CASE WHEN [bolCurrent] = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 2 END AS [Sort], 
		tblFTdocs.EntryDate AS EnteredDate, 
		tblFTdocs.EntryBy AS EnteredBy, 
		E.[First Name] AS EnteredByGivenName, 
		E.Surname AS EnteredBySurname, 
		Left(ISNULL([E].[First Name],''),1) AS EnteredByGivenNameInitial, 
		Left(ISNULL([Surname],''),1) AS EnteredBySurnameInitial
	FROM tblFTdocs LEFT JOIN tblEmployees AS E ON tblFTdocs.EntryBy = E.[Employee Code];


-- dbo.zsqmlFTEquipment_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlFTEquipment_SQL]
AS

	SELECT   
		tblFTequip.SeqNo,
		tblFTequip.TicketId,
		tblFTequip.EquipId,
		tlkpFTequip.[Desc] AS EquipDesc, 
        tlkpBillingRates.txtUnit AS UsageUnit,
        CASE WHEN [UseDay] = 1 THEN [Usage] ELSE [EquipTime] END AS UsageQty, 
        CASE 
			WHEN [UseDay] = 1 THEN 
				CASE WHEN [Usage] = 1 THEN 'Full' ELSE 
					CASE WHEN [Usage] = .5 THEN '1/2' ELSE '' END END
			ELSE CONVERT(VARCHAR(10), [EquipTime]) END AS UsageQtyNamed, 
        REPLACE(ISNULL(tblFTequip.Owner, ''), '~', ', ') AS Owners, 
        tblFTequip.NumUnits AS EquipCount, 
        tlkpFTequip.CpyWorkType AS WorkTypeCoy,
		tlkpFTequip.EmpWorkType AS WorkTypeEmp,
		tblFTequip.OrderNo, 
        tblFTequip.ChargeAmt,
		tlkpFTstyleEquip.ChargeGrp,
		FT.Status
	FROM
	        ((((tblFTequip INNER JOIN tlkpFTequip ON tblFTequip.EquipId = tlkpFTequip.EquipId)
                   INNER JOIN tblFieldTicket ON tblFTequip.TicketId = tblFieldTicket.TicketId)
                  LEFT JOIN tlkpFTstyleEquip ON (tlkpFTequip.EquipId = tlkpFTstyleEquip.EquipId) AND
                                                 (tblFieldTicket.TicketStyle = tlkpFTstyleEquip.TicketStyle))
                 INNER JOIN tlkpFTstyle ON tblFieldTicket.TicketStyle = tlkpFTstyle.TicketStyle)
                LEFT JOIN tlkpBillingRates ON (tlkpFTstyle.DisbEmpCode = tlkpBillingRates.[Employee Code]) AND
                                               (tlkpFTequip.CpyWorkType = tlkpBillingRates.[Work Type])
	
	INNER JOIN tblFieldTicket FT ON FT.TicketId = tblFTequip.TicketId 
	
	
	WHERE
		( 
			(tlkpFTstyleEquip.ChargeGrp IS NOT NULL AND tblFTequip.ChargeAmt > 0 AND FT.Status LIKE '%Approved%') OR 
			(FT.Status LIKE '%Submitted%') OR 
			(FT.Status LIKE '%Draft%') OR 
			 tlkpFTstyleEquip.ChargeGrp IS NULL 
		)
		
		
	--ORDER BY TicketId, SeqNo;


-- dbo.zsqmlFTHiddenCalcs_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlFTHiddenCalcs_SQL]
AS
SELECT zstmpFThiddenCalcs.SeqNo, zstmpFThiddenCalcs.WTdesc, zstmpFThiddenCalcs.Qty, zstmpFThiddenCalcs.CostAmt, zstmpFThiddenCalcs.ChargeAmt, 
       zstmpFThiddenCalcs.TicketId
FROM zstmpFThiddenCalcs;


-- dbo.zsqmlFTSupply_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlFTSupply_SQL]
AS

	SELECT 
		tblFTsupply.SeqNo, 
		tblFTsupply.TicketId, 
		tblFTsupply.ItemId, 
		tlkpFTsupply.[Desc] AS ItemDesc, 
		tlkpFTsupply.WorkType AS ItemWorkType, 
		tblFTsupply.Amount, 
		tblFTsupply.OrderNo,
		tlkpBillingRates.txtUnit AS Unit
	FROM tblFTsupply 
	INNER JOIN tlkpFTsupply ON tblFTsupply.ItemId = tlkpFTsupply.ItemId
	INNER JOIN tblFieldTicket ON tblFTsupply.TicketId = tblFieldTicket.TicketId
	INNER JOIN tlkpFTstyle ON tblFieldTicket.TicketStyle = tlkpFTstyle.TicketStyle
	INNER JOIN tlkpBillingRates ON (tlkpFTsupply.WorkType = tlkpBillingRates.[Work Type]) AND (tlkpBillingRates.[Employee Code] = tlkpFTstyle.DisbEmpCode);


-- dbo.zsqmlFTTimeAndExpense_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlFTTimeAndExpense_SQL]
AS

	SELECT 
		tblFTtime.TicketId,
		tblFTtime.EmpCode, 
		E.[First Name] AS EmployeeGivenName, 
		Left(ISNULL([E].[First Name],''),1) AS EmployeeGivenNameInitial, 
		E.Surname AS EmployeeSurname, 
		Left(ISNULL([Surname],''),1) AS EmployeeSurnameInitial, 
		tblFTtime.CrewRole, 
		CASE WHEN [tblFTtime].[CrewRole]='C' THEN 'Crew Chief' ELSE 'Assistant' END AS CrewRoleName, 
		CASE WHEN [tblFTtime].[CrewRole]='C' THEN 1 ELSE 2 END AS Sort, 
		Min(CASE WHEN [TimeCol]=1 THEN [TimeQty] ELSE Null END) AS TimeQty1, 
		Min(CASE WHEN [TimeCol]=1 THEN [TimeQtyApprvd] ELSE Null END) AS TimeQty1Approved, 
		Min(CASE WHEN [TimeCol]=2 THEN [TimeQty] ELSE Null END) AS TimeQty2, 
		Min(CASE WHEN [TimeCol]=2 THEN [TimeQtyApprvd] ELSE Null END) AS TimeQty2Approved, 
		Min(CASE WHEN [TimeCol]=3 THEN [TimeQty] ELSE Null END) AS TimeQty3, 
		Min(CASE WHEN [TimeCol]=3 THEN [TimeQtyApprvd] ELSE Null END) AS TimeQty3Approved, 
		Min(CASE WHEN [TimeCol]=4 THEN [TimeQty] ELSE Null END) AS TimeQty4, 
		Min(CASE WHEN [TimeCol]=4 THEN [TimeQtyApprvd] ELSE Null END) AS TimeQty4Approved, 
		Min(CASE WHEN [TimeCol]=5 THEN [TimeQty] ELSE Null END) AS TimeQty5, 
		Min(CASE WHEN [TimeCol]=5 THEN [TimeQtyApprvd] ELSE Null END) AS TimeQty5Approved, 
		Sum([TimeQty]) AS TimeQtyTotal,
		Sum([TimeQtyApprvd]) AS TimeQtyTotalApproved,
		Min(CASE WHEN [StdExpCol]=1 THEN [StdExpQty] ELSE Null END) AS ExpenseQty1, 
		Min(CASE WHEN [StdExpCol]=1 THEN [StdExpQtyApprvd] ELSE Null END) AS ExpenseQty1Approved, 
		Min(CASE WHEN [StdExpCol]=2 THEN [StdExpQty] ELSE Null END) AS ExpenseQty2, 
		Min(CASE WHEN [StdExpCol]=2 THEN [StdExpQtyApprvd] ELSE Null END) AS ExpenseQty2Approved, 
		Min(CASE WHEN [StdExpCol]=3 THEN [StdExpQty] ELSE Null END) AS ExpenseQty3, 
		Min(CASE WHEN [StdExpCol]=3 THEN [StdExpQtyApprvd] ELSE Null END) AS ExpenseQty3Approved, 
		Min(CASE WHEN [StdExpCol]=4 THEN [StdExpQty] ELSE Null END) AS ExpenseQty4, 
		Min(CASE WHEN [StdExpCol]=4 THEN [StdExpQtyApprvd] ELSE Null END) AS ExpenseQty4Approved, 
		Min(CASE WHEN [StdExpCol]=5 THEN [StdExpQty] ELSE Null END) AS ExpenseQty5, 
		Min(CASE WHEN [StdExpCol]=5 THEN [StdExpQtyApprvd] ELSE Null END) AS ExpenseQty5Approved,
		Sum([StdExpQty]) AS ExpenseQtyTotal,
		Sum([StdExpQtyApprvd]) AS ExpenseQtyTotalApproved
	FROM tblFTtime 
	INNER JOIN tblFTstdExp ON tblFTtime.SeqNo = tblFTstdExp.SeqNo
	INNER JOIN tblEmployees AS E ON tblFTtime.EmpCode = E.[Employee Code]
	GROUP BY 
		tblFTtime.TicketId,
		tblFTtime.EmpCode, 
		E.[First Name], 
		--Left(Nz([E].[First Name],''),1), 
		E.Surname,
		--Left(Nz([Surname],''),1), 
		tblFTtime.CrewRole
		--IIf([tblFTtime].[CrewRole]='C','Crew Chief','Assistant');


-- dbo.zsqmlFT_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlFT_SQL]
AS
	SELECT 
		tblFIeldTicket.TicketId, 
		tblFIeldTicket.TicketNo, 
		tblFIeldTicket.TicketDate, 
		tblFIeldTicket.TicketStyle, 
		tblFIeldTicket.Status, 
		tblFIeldTicket.JobNo, 
		tblFIeldTicket.TaskNo, 
		tblFIeldTicket.CrewChief, 
		tblFIeldTicket.ClientFieldRep, 
		tblFIeldTicket.ClientCost, 
		tblFIeldTicket.SiteDesc, 
		tblFIeldTicket.WorkDesc, 
		tblFIeldTicket.WorkDescApprvd, 
		tblFIeldTicket.Conditions, 
		tblFIeldTicket.TravelTo, 
		tblFIeldTicket.LDKey, 
		tblFIeldTicket.SubJobNo, 
		CR1.ClientRefNo AS ClientRef1, 
		CR1.ClientRefTypeName AS ClientRef1TypeName, 
		CR2.ClientRefNo AS ClientRef2, 
		CR2.ClientRefTypeName AS ClientRef2TypeName, 
		CR3.ClientRefNo AS ClientRef3, 
		CR3.ClientRefTypeName AS ClientRef3TypeName, 
		CR4.ClientRefNo AS ClientRef4, 
		CR4.ClientRefTypeName AS ClientRef4TypeName, 
		CR5.ClientRefNo AS ClientRef5, 
		CR5.ClientRefTypeName AS ClientRef5TypeName, 
		E.[First Name] AS CrewChiefGivenName, 
		E.Surname AS CrewChiefSurname, 
		Left(ISNULL([E].[First Name],''),1) AS CrewChiefGivenNameInitial, 
		Left(ISNULL([E].[Surname],''),1) AS CrewChiefSurnameInitial,
		J.[Client]
	FROM tblFIeldTicket 
	INNER JOIN tblJobs AS J ON J.[Job Number] = tblFieldTicket.JobNo
	LEFT JOIN zsqmlClientRef_SQL AS CR1 ON tblFIeldTicket.ClientRef1 = CR1.ClientRefId
	LEFT JOIN zsqmlClientRef_SQL AS CR2 ON tblFIeldTicket.ClientRef2 = CR2.ClientRefId
	LEFT JOIN zsqmlClientRef_SQL AS CR3 ON tblFIeldTicket.ClientRef3 = CR3.ClientRefId
	LEFT JOIN zsqmlClientRef_SQL AS CR4 ON tblFIeldTicket.ClientRef4 = CR4.ClientRefId
	LEFT JOIN zsqmlClientRef_SQL AS CR5 ON tblFIeldTicket.ClientRef5 = CR5.ClientRefId
	LEFT JOIN tblEmployees AS E ON tblFIeldTicket.CrewChief = E.[Employee Code];

					  ClientRefNo2 = ( SELECT [ClientRefNo] FROM tblClientRefs WHERE ClientRefId = dbo.tblClientsInvoices.ClientRef2 ),
					  ClientRefNo3 = ( SELECT [ClientRefNo] FROM tblClientRefs WHERE ClientRefId = dbo.tblClientsInvoices.ClientRef3 ),
					  ClientRefNo4 = ( SELECT [ClientRefNo] FROM tblClientRefs WHERE ClientRefId = dbo.tblClientsInvoices.ClientRef4 ),
					  ClientRefNo5 = ( SELECT [ClientRefNo] FROM tblClientRefs WHERE ClientRefId = dbo.tblClientsInvoices.ClientRef5 ),
					  dbo.tblClientsInvoices.TaskNo,					  
					  BillingClientCode = dbo.tblClientsInvoices.strBillingClientCode,
					  BillingClientName = ( SELECT [Company Name] FROM tblClients WHERE [Client Code] = dbo.tblClientsInvoices.strBillingClientCode ),
					  PostalAddrLine1 = (SELECT [Data] FROM dbo.fnLA_Explode(dbo.tblClientsInvoices.[txtPostalAddress]) WHERE ID = 1),
					  PostalAddrLine2 = (SELECT [Data] FROM dbo.fnLA_Explode(dbo.tblClientsInvoices.[txtPostalAddress]) WHERE ID = 2),
					  PostalAddrLine3 = (SELECT [Data] FROM dbo.fnLA_Explode(dbo.tblClientsInvoices.[txtPostalAddress]) WHERE ID = 3),
					  PostalAddrLine4 = (SELECT [Data] FROM dbo.fnLA_Explode(dbo.tblClientsInvoices.[txtPostalAddress]) WHERE ID = 4),
					  PostalAddrLine5 = (SELECT [Data] FROM dbo.fnLA_Explode(dbo.tblClientsInvoices.[txtPostalAddress]) WHERE ID = 5),  					  
                      PayTermsText = CASE ISNULL(dbo.tblClientsInvoices.strPaymentTerms, '0')
						WHEN '0' THEN 'Due Upon Receipt'
						ELSE dbo.tblClientsInvoices.strPaymentTerms
					  END
FROM         dbo.tblClientsInvoices CROSS JOIN
                      dbo.zstblSetup
ORDER BY dbo.tblClientsInvoices.txtClientCode, dbo.tblClientsInvoices.txtJobNumber, dbo.tblClientsInvoices.dteInvoiceDate, dbo.tblClientsInvoices.lngInvoiceNo;


-- dbo.zsqmlJobQuotes_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlJobQuotes_SQL]
AS
SELECT     dbo.tblJobsQuote.JQJobNo, dbo.tblJobsQuote.JQCode, dbo.tblJobsQuote.JQDesc, dbo.tblJobsQuote.JQInactive, dbo.tblJobsQuoteLines.QLDesc, 
                      dbo.tblJobsQuoteLines.QLHours, dbo.tblJobsQuoteLines.QLCost, dbo.tblJobsQuoteLines.QLCharge, dbo.tblJobsQuoteLines.QLAmount
FROM         dbo.tblJobsQuote INNER JOIN
                      dbo.tblJobsQuoteLines ON dbo.tblJobsQuote.JQKey = dbo.tblJobsQuoteLines.QLJQKey
WHERE     (dbo.tblJobsQuote.JQInactive = 0);


-- dbo.zsqmlJobReference_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlJobReference_SQL]
AS
SELECT     strJobReference, strRe, Details AS RefDetails, strRe AS Ref1, strRe AS Ref2
FROM         dbo.tblRegister
WHERE     (strRegisterType = 'Reference') AND (ISNULL(strRe, N'') <> '');


-- dbo.zsqmlJobs_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlJobs_SQL]
AS
SELECT TOP(100) PERCENT J.*,

	CaptainName = LTRIM(RTRIM(ISNULL(dbo.tblEmployees.[First Name], '') + ' ' + ISNULL(dbo.tblEmployees.Surname, ''))), 
	CaptainGivenName = dbo.tblEmployees.[First Name],
	CaptainGivenNameInitial = LEFT(dbo.tblEmployees.[First Name], 1),
	CaptainSurname = dbo.tblEmployees.Surname,
	CaptainSurnameInitial = LEFT(dbo.tblEmployees.Surname, 1),
		
	SubCaptainName = LTRIM(RTRIM(ISNULL(tblEmployees_1.[First Name], '') + ' ' + ISNULL(tblEmployees_1.Surname, ''))), 
	SubCaptainGivenName = tblEmployees_1.[First Name],
	SubCaptainGivenNameInitial = LEFT(tblEmployees_1.[First Name], 1),
	SubCaptainSurname = tblEmployees_1.Surname,
	SubCaptainSurnameInitial = LEFT(tblEmployees_1.Surname, 1),

	EnteredByGivenName = ENTERED.[First Name],
	EnteredByGivenNameInitial = LEFT(ENTERED.[First Name], 1),
	EnteredBySurname = ENTERED.[Surname],
	EnteredBySurnameInitial = LEFT(ENTERED.[Surname], 1),
		
	InspTitle = insp.ContactSalutation,
	InspGivenName = insp.ContactGivenName,
	InspGivenNameInitial = LEFT(insp.ContactGivenName, 1),          
	InspSurname = insp.ContactSurname,
	InspSurnameInitial = LEFT(insp.ContactSurname, 1),
	InspPhone = insp.ContactPhone, 
	InspMobile = insp.ContactMobile, 
	InspFax = insp.ContactFax, 
	InspEmail = insp.ContactEMail,

	BillTitle = bill.ContactSalutation,
	BillGivenName = bill.ContactGivenName,
	BillGivenNameInitial = LEFT(bill.ContactGivenName, 1),
	BillSurname = bill.ContactSurname,
	BillSurnameInitial = LEFT(bill.ContactSurname, 1),
    BillName = LTRIM(RTRIM(ISNULL(bill.ContactSalutation, '') + ' ' + ISNULL(bill.ContactGivenName, '') + ' ' + ISNULL(bill.ContactSurname, ''))), 
    BillPhone = bill.ContactPhone, 
    BillMobile = bill.ContactMobile, 
    BillFax = bill.ContactFax, 
    BillEmail = bill.ContactEMail, 

	BillAddr = dbo.fnLA_AssembleAddress('Billing', 'Postal Address', J.[Job Number], NULL, 0)
	
FROM         dbo.tblJobs AS J
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.tblEmployees ON J.strCaptainCode = dbo.tblEmployees.[Employee Code] 
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.tblEmployees AS tblEmployees_1 ON J.strSubCaptain = tblEmployees_1.[Employee Code] 
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.tblEmployees AS ENTERED ON J.EnteredBy = ENTERED.[Employee Code] 
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.tblClientsContacts AS insp ON J.InstructingPersonId = insp.ContactID 
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.tblClientsContacts AS bill ON J.JobBillingContactId = bill.ContactID;


-- dbo.zsqmlLegalDescLegalParcel_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlLegalDescLegalParcel_SQL]
AS
SELECT   
	LDKey, 
	dbo.fnLA_GetLegalDesc(LDKey) AS LDdesc, 
	JobNo, 
	[Desc] AS Note,
	UsageText = CASE Usage 
		WHEN 'Main' THEN 'Start'
		WHEN 'Bottom' THEN 'End'
		ELSE Usage
	END,	
	UsageSort = CASE Usage 
		WHEN 'Main' THEN 1
		WHEN 'Bottom' THEN 2
		ELSE 3
	END	
FROM dbo.tblLegalDescJob
WHERE
	(Usage <> 'New') OR (Usage IS NULL);

-- dbo.zsqmlQuotes_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlQuotes_SQL]
AS
SELECT TOP(100) PERCENT 
	J.[Client], 
	JQ.JQKey, 
	JQ.JQCode, 
	JQ.JQJobNo, 
	JQ.JQDesc, 
	JQ.JQCreated, 
	JQ.JQUpdated, 
	JQ.JQValidTo, 
	JQ.JQComments, 
	JQ.JQInactive, 
	JQ.JQLinked, 
	JQ.JQDfltTaxId, 
	JQ.JQDfltTaxTerritory, 
	JQ.JQDfltTaxCboId, 
	JQ.JQDate, 
	JQ.JQFrom, 
	JQ.JQFromGivenName, 
	JQ.JQFromSurname,
	JQ.JQTo,
	JQ.JQToAddr,
	ToClientName = ( SELECT [Company Name] FROM tblClients WHERE [Client Code] = JQ.JQTo ),
	ToAddrLine1 = (SELECT [Data] FROM dbo.fnLA_Explode(JQ.[JQToAddr]) WHERE ID = 1),
	ToAddrLine2 = (SELECT [Data] FROM dbo.fnLA_Explode(JQ.[JQToAddr]) WHERE ID = 2),
	ToAddrLine3 = (SELECT [Data] FROM dbo.fnLA_Explode(JQ.[JQToAddr]) WHERE ID = 3),
	ToAddrLine4 = (SELECT [Data] FROM dbo.fnLA_Explode(JQ.[JQToAddr]) WHERE ID = 4),
	ToAddrLine5 = (SELECT [Data] FROM dbo.fnLA_Explode(JQ.[JQToAddr]) WHERE ID = 5), 	
	Expr1 =	JQ.upsize_ts, 
	Z.*

FROM         dbo.vwLA_qryQuoteFromName  AS JQ CROSS JOIN
                      dbo.zstblSetup AS Z INNER JOIN dbo.tblJobs J
                           ON JQ.JQJobNo = J.[Job Number];

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlRegisterSetupData_SQL]
AS
SELECT     dbo.tblRegister.Counter, dbo.tblRegister.[File Number], dbo.tblRegister.Details, dbo.tblRegister.strRegisterType, dbo.tblRegister.strJobReference,

-- dbo.zsqmlRegisterTransmittal_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlRegisterTransmittal_SQL]
AS
SELECT     dbo.tblRegisterHistory.cntRegHistCounter, dbo.tblRegister.Counter, dbo.tblRegister.dteRegisterDate, dbo.tblRegisterHistory.numCopies, 
                      dbo.tblRegisterHistory.txtCopyType, dbo.tblRegister.strRe, dbo.tblRegisterHistory.strMethod, dbo.tblRegister.strJobReference, 
                      dbo.vwLA_qryJobCaptain.[Job Description], dbo.vwLA_qryJobCaptain.Contact, dbo.tblClients.[Company Name] AS ClientName, 
                      LTRIM(RTRIM(ISNULL(C.ContactGivenName, '') + ' ' + ISNULL(C.ContactSurname, ''))) AS Attention, dbo.tblClients.Category
FROM         dbo.tblRegister INNER JOIN
                      dbo.vwLA_qryJobCaptain ON dbo.tblRegister.strJobReference = dbo.vwLA_qryJobCaptain.[Job Number] INNER JOIN
                      dbo.tblRegisterHistory INNER JOIN
                      dbo.vwLA_qryContacts AS C ON dbo.tblRegisterHistory.strTo = C.ContactIDStr INNER JOIN
                      dbo.tblClients ON C.ClientId = dbo.tblClients.[Client Code] ON dbo.tblRegister.Counter = dbo.tblRegisterHistory.lngRegCounter
GROUP BY dbo.tblRegisterHistory.cntRegHistCounter, dbo.tblRegister.Counter, dbo.tblRegister.dteRegisterDate, dbo.tblRegisterHistory.numCopies, 
                      dbo.tblRegisterHistory.txtCopyType, dbo.tblRegister.strRe, dbo.tblRegisterHistory.strMethod, dbo.tblRegister.strJobReference, 
                      dbo.vwLA_qryJobCaptain.[Job Description], dbo.vwLA_qryJobCaptain.Contact, dbo.tblClients.[Company Name], C.ContactGivenName, C.ContactSurname, 
                      dbo.tblClients.Category;


-- dbo.zsqmlStatement_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlStatement_SQL]
AS
SELECT tblClients.*, zstblSetup.Address AS MAddr, zstblSetup.strCompanyEmail AS MEMail, zstblSetup.Fax AS MFax, zstblSetup.oleLetterHead AS MLetterHead, zstblSetup.oleLogo1 AS MLogo1, zstblSetup.oleLogo2 AS MLogo2, zstblSetup.[Company Name] AS MName, zstblSetup.strCompanyNumber AS MNumber, zstblSetup.strOtherCompanyNumber AS MOtherNumber, zstblSetup.PartnersAssociates AS MPartAssocs, zstblSetup.Phone AS MPhone, zstblSetup.[Postal Address] AS MPostalAddr, zstblSetup.CompanySpecialities AS MSpecial, zstblSetup.strCompanyWEB AS MWeb
FROM tblClients, zstblSetup;


-- dbo.zsqmlTask_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlTask_SQL]
AS
SELECT     
	T.[Task No], 
	T.[Job Code], 
	T.[Employee Code], 
	T.[Parent Task No], 
	T.[Completion %], 
	T.[Date Started], 
	T.[Date Expected], 
	T.[Date Completed], 
	T.[Task Description], 
	T.[Task Type], 
	T.[Date Entered], 
	T.lngPhoneMessageRef, 
	T.strWhoEntered, 
	T.strJobNoteRef, 
	T.strSeqNo, 
	T.curActCost, 
	T.curActCharge, 
	T.bolShowOnQuote, 
	T.memQuoteText, 
	T.curEstCost, 
	T.curEstCharge, 
	T.strWorkType, 
	T.EnteredBy, 
	T.intEstHrs, 
	T.intActHrs, 
	T.TaskCode, 
	T.strTaskName, 
	T.strTaskStatus, 
	T.strResourceType, 
	T.dteExpectedStart, 
	T.curEstCostRate, 
	T.curEstRate, 
	T.curActCostRate, 
	T.curActRate, 
	T.bolIncludeInQuote, 
	T.ParentSeq, 
	T.TaskSeqNo, 
	T.SeqLevel, 
	T.LastChildSeq, 
	T.IsSummary, 
	T.upsize_ts, 
	T.bolFixedPrice, 
	T.ActCalcSrc, 
	ResourceName = LTRIM(RTRIM(ISNULL(dbo.tblEmployees.[First Name], N'') + ' ' + ISNULL(dbo.tblEmployees.Surname, N'')))
	
FROM         dbo.tblJobsNotes AS T LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.tblEmployees ON T.[Employee Code] = dbo.tblEmployees.[Employee Code];


-- dbo.zsqmlTeam_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlTeam_SQL]
AS
SELECT     
	dbo.tblJobsContacts.JobNumber, 
	dbo.tblJobsContacts.ContactID, 
	dbo.tblJobsContacts.ContactRole, 
	dbo.tblJobsContacts.ClientCode, 
	dbo.tblClients.[Company Name], 
	ContactName = LTRIM(RTRIM(ISNULL(dbo.tblClientsContacts.ContactSalutation, '') + ' ' + 
							  ISNULL(dbo.tblClientsContacts.ContactGivenName, '')  + ' ' + 
							  ISNULL(dbo.tblClientsContacts.ContactSurname, ''))), 
	dbo.tblClientsContacts.ContactPhone, 
	dbo.tblClientsContacts.ContactMobile,
	dbo.tblClientsContacts.ContactFax, 
	dbo.tblCLientsContacts.ContactEmail
	
FROM         dbo.tblClientsContacts INNER JOIN
                      dbo.tblJobsContacts INNER JOIN
                      dbo.tblClients ON dbo.tblJobsContacts.ClientCode = dbo.tblClients.[Client Code] ON dbo.tblClientsContacts.ContactID = dbo.tblJobsContacts.ContactID;


-- dbo.zsqmlTimesheetsSortByDateDesc_SQL source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[zsqmlTimesheetsSortByDateDesc_SQL]
AS
SELECT     TOP (100) PERCENT 
	T.[TimeSheet Number], 
	T.[Employee Code], 
	T.Date, 
	T.[Job Number], 
	T.[Work Type], 
	T.[Hours Worked], 
	T.[Hourly Rate], 
	T.[Work Description], 
	T.Extension, 
	T.[Job Description], 
	T.TDate, 
	T.ApptTime, 
	T.Status, 
	T.ApptDate, 
	T.lngInvoiceNo, 
	T.txtUnit, 
	T.curCostRate, 
	T.curCostsExtension, 
	T.tmeStart, 
	T.tmeEnd, 
	T.strJobNoteRef, 
	T.bolDisbursement, 
	T.bolNonChargeable, 
	T.sglFactor, 
	T.strTaskType, 
	T.PayTypeKey, 
	T.bolShow, 
	T.TaskCode, 
	T.lngInvoiceNoDraft, 
	T.PayExportDate, 
	T.OTclaim, 
	T.upsize_ts, 
	T.InvTSGroup, 
	T.TsSrc, 
	T.sngWorkTime,
	
	WT.[Work Type Description], 
	WT.[WorkTypeLongDesc]
	
FROM         dbo.tblTimesheets AS T
LEFT JOIN tlkpWorkTypes AS WT ON WT.[Work Type Code] = T.[Work Type]
WHERE     (T.bolDisbursement = 0 OR T.bolDisbursement IS NULL)
ORDER BY T.Date DESC;
